SECTION 13: SCHEMA MANAGER
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

showDeviceDataUi() → 700x800 modeless dialog in 'schema' mode.

Schema is stored as a JSON array in DocumentProperties under 'SCHEMA_CONFIG_ARRAY'.
Falls back to DEFAULT_SCHEMA_ARRAY if missing/corrupt.

getSchemaConfig() / saveSchemaConfig(newArray) / resetSchemaToDefaults()
resetSchemaToDefaults(): confirm dialog clarifies "resets column definitions only — sheet data not affected".

SCHEMA MODAL UI (schemaContainer, #schemaBody):
  Close button: btn-mono (matches all other modals).
  Add-row inputs: "Field key (e.g. rack_id)" + "Display label" placeholders.
  Footer (modal-actions, 3 footer-groups, ui-equal-size=128px):
    Left:   Reset Defaults (btn-danger)
    Center: "Apply Formatting" checkbox (chkApplyFormatting, title explains connection
            colors/conditional rules/MLAG borders/speed coding) + Check Sync (SVG
            magnifier) + Force Sync (SVG refresh)
    Right:  Save & Sync (btn-success, orange+asterisk when dirty, green when clean)
  Footer buttons use inline SVG icons (13×13) — no emoji.
  modified-highlight: border-bottom 2px solid #f59e0b + background rgba(245,158,11,0.08)
    (dark-mode compatible; previously hardcoded #fffbeb cream).

Schema columns can be:
  - Reordered (affects sheet column order after sync)
  - Have custom dropdown options added/removed
  - Have columns added (custom attributes)
  - Have columns deleted (with orphan safety prompt during sync)

syncSchemaPreservingOrder(optionalForcedSchema, applyFormatting, deleteOrphans):
  Main sync function. deleteOrphans: true=delete orphaned cols, false=keep, null=ui.alert fallback.
  Callers (triggerSyncOnly, saveSchemaChanges) pre-check via getOrphanedColumnsInfo() and
  pass explicit deleteOrphans so the sidebar loading overlay never hides the prompt.
  Then calls rebuildSheet() to apply the new structure.

auditSchemaVsSheet():
  Returns { extra, missing, conflicts } comparing expected headers vs actual.
  conflict detection is done client-side (conflicts array is always empty from server).
  IMPORTANT: actualHeaders filters out DUMMY_VIS_HEADER (_sys_) before comparison,
  so the system column is never flagged as "Extra" in the Column Sync status.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 14: COLUMN VISIBILITY (VIEW MODES)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SYSTEM VISIBILITY COLUMN (_sys_):
  DUMMY_VIS_HEADER = '_sys_' constant in Code.gs.
  _sys_ is ALWAYS VISIBLE at col A — never hidden. Eliminates all "can't hide all columns"
  GAS errors. Col A stays clean (no bullet markers written — col is empty except headers).
  On creation, ensureDummyColumn sets:
    - Row 1, col 1: '↕' (hint label)
    - Row 2, col 1: '_sys_' (detection header)
    - Cell note: 'Managed by TopoAssist — do not edit. This column tracks row visibility
      and is required for the hide/show feature to work correctly.'
    - Column width: 36px
  ensureDummyColumn(sheet): ensures _sys_ exists at col 1. No hide logic.
    - If col 1 header already equals _sys_: skips insert but still applies gray styling.
    - Otherwise: insertColumnBefore(1), sets headers/note/width, then applies gray styling.
    - Always sets background #e2e8f0 on rows 1..max(lastRow,3) of col 1 so the column is
      visually marked as reserved regardless of whether it was just created or already existed.
  _applyDeviceCols() — REMOVED. toggleSheetDevice now uses applyCustomView(getViewPreferences())
    for both hide and show, same as column toggle. This ensures device show/hide respects the
    current column type view without stale mode-string logic.
  refreshSheetRowVisibility(): calls ensureDummyColumn() FIRST (before reading headers),
    then re-reads lastCol and headers. Scans visible int_ columns; computes toShow/toHide
    row lists; hides/shows rows via _batchRowOp(). Does NOT write anything to col A.
  Device columns always start at col 2+. applyCustomView skips col 1 (_sys_) via colIdx===1 guard.

viewShowAll():
  Calls saveSheetViewHidden([]) + applyCustomView(all schema keys) + refreshSheetRowVisibility().
  Clears all Sheet View hidden devices AND shows all column types AND refreshes row visibility.
  Menu label: "Show All Columns/Devices".

Sheet View menu items — all use applyCustomView() (same as Sheet View panel):
  viewCabling()     → applyCustomView(['int'])                              + showSheetAssistPanel()
  viewTransceiver() → applyCustomView(['int','xcvr'])                       + showSheetAssistPanel()
  viewSpeed()       → applyCustomView(['int','xcvr','et_speed','xcvr_speed'])+ showSheetAssistPanel()
  viewPo()          → applyCustomView(['int','po'])                         + showSheetAssistPanel()
  viewMode()        → applyCustomView(['int','po','sp_mode'])               + showSheetAssistPanel()
  viewVlan()        → applyCustomView(['int','po','sp_mode','vlan'])        + showSheetAssistPanel()

  Sidebar presets (loadViewPreset in Sidebar-js.html) mirror these 6 keys:
    cabling / transceiver / speed / po / mode / vlan

setColumnVisibility() — REMOVED. All callers now use applyCustomView().
  showAllSheetDevices(): saveSheetViewHidden([]) + applyCustomView(getViewPreferences()) + refresh
  hideAllSheetDevices(): saveSheetViewHidden(all) + applyCustomView(getViewPreferences()) + refresh

Custom View (merged into SheetAssistPanel.html right column):
  - No longer a separate dialog; now the right column of the Sheet View panel (490×420).
  - SHOW ALL / HIDE ALL buttons — same style as device panel; no presets.
  - Key mapping used by menu view functions:
      cabling → ['int']
      po      → ['int', 'po']
      mode    → ['int', 'po', 'sp_mode']
      vlan    → ['int', 'po', 'vlan']
      xcvr    → ['int', 'xcvr']
  - applyCustomView(selectedKeys):
      A. Saves selectedKeys to CUSTOM_VIEW_PREFS (UserProperties) + SHEET_VIEW_MODE='CUSTOM'.
      B. Reads row-2 headers; computes target[i] (true=show, false=hide) per column:
           col 1 (_sys_) → always true
           column type:  header must start with one of selectedKeys + '_'
           device:       header must NOT end with '_' + a hiddenDevs entry
      C. Applies show/hide in batched consecutive runs (NO blanket showColumns reset) to
         avoid the all-columns-expand flash — each run calls
         sheet.showColumns(start, count) or sheet.hideColumns(start, count) once.
      Does NOT call showSheetAssistPanel() — panel callers keep the panel open; menu callers
      (viewIntOnly etc.) call showSheetAssistPanel() explicitly after applyCustomView.
  - showCustomViewUi() is DEAD CODE in Code.gs — no callers exist anywhere; menu item calls showSheetAssistPanel() instead. Safe to delete.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 15: SNAPSHOTS / CHECKPOINTS
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

createTopologySnapshot():
  - Prompts user for a name via ui.prompt()
  - Creates tab named SNAP_<unixMs>_<safeName>
  - Rows 1-2 = metadata; rows 3+ = original sheet content (formulas → static)
  - Tab color: orange

getSnapshotList():
  - Returns [{name, label, dateStr}] — newest first
  - label = parts after SNAP_<ts>_ joined by underscore
  - dateStr = new Date(ts).toLocaleString()

getSnapshotDiff(snapshotName):
  - Snapshot structure: row 1-2 = metadata, row 3 = device names,
    row 4 = int_ headers, rows 5+ = data
  - Reads live row 2 and snapshot row 4 for device list (int_ headers)
  - Data comparison: live rows 3+ vs snapshot rows 5+ (overlapping area)
  - Returns: { devicesAdded, devicesRemoved, liveDataRows, snapDataRows,
               changedCells, rowDelta }

showRestoreWizard():
  - 420x430 GAS modal dialog (separate from Sidebar.html modal system)
  - Dropdown shows "${label} — ${dateStr}" per snapshot
  - On dropdown change: calls getSnapshotDiff() via google.script.run
  - Diff panel shows row counts, delta (color-coded), changed cells,
    devices added/removed
  - Restore button DISABLED until diff loads successfully
  - On restore: calls restoreFromSnapshot(), closes on success

restoreFromSnapshot(snapshotName):
  - Reads snapshot from row 3 onward (skips 2 metadata rows)
  - Validates snapData is non-empty BEFORE touching live sheet
  - Backs up current live sheet; then clears + writes snapshot data
  - Calls syncSchemaPreservingOrder() to re-apply formatting
  - On any error: rolls back live backup; throws with rollback status in message
  - INVARIANT: live sheet must never be left empty due to a failed restore

showNewProjectDialog():
  - 400x330 GAS modal dialog (HtmlService, separate from Sidebar modal system)
  - Shows a red warning box: data will be permanently erased
  - Checkbox "Keep one device as starting point" (default: checked)
  - Device name text input (default: "Spine1"), hidden when checkbox unchecked
  - "Reset & Start New Project" (red) + "Cancel" buttons
  - On confirm: calls resetToNewProject(keepDevice, deviceName)

resetToNewProject(keepDevice, deviceName):
  - Gets the working sheet by SHEET_DATA name; throws if not found
  - Validates deviceName regex BEFORE clearing (avoids clear+fail leaving blank sheet)
  - Backs up live data; calls sheet.clear(); then optionally rebuildSheet()
  - If keepDevice=true: rebuildSheet([{name: deviceName, type: 'full'}], null, false)
    creates a fresh one-device structure with default schema
  - If keepDevice=false: leaves sheet empty (intentional new-project reset)
  - On any error: rolls back live backup; throws with rollback status in message
  - INVARIANT: if rebuild fails, original data is restored; sheet never stays blank unexpectedly

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 16: AUDIT / VALIDATION ENGINE
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Client-side in Sidebar-js.html: runValidation() / toggleValidationMode()

Audit checks (runValidation() in Sidebar-js.html):

CHECK GROUP 1 — Link-based (per-link in globalLinks):
  A. Po Mismatch — both sides have po_ set but to different values
       → flagErrorOnPort on both link.u and link.v
       msg: "✗ Po Mismatch: DevA has Po1 but DevB has Po2"
  B. Po Asymmetry — one side has po_ set, peer has po_ blank
       → flagErrorOnPort on both ports
       msg: "✗ Po Asymmetry: DevA has Po1 but peer has no po_ set"
  C. MLAG Destination — same Po number points to different remote device names
  D. VLAN Mismatch — vlan_ values differ across a cable (Arista-only links)
  E. Mode Incompatible — sp_mode_ pair is not in VALID_MODE_PAIRS
  F. Speed Mismatch — et_speed_ values differ across a cable (Arista-only links)
       Skips blank and 'auto'. Direct comparison only: 25g ↔ 10g flagged, 25g ↔ 25g passes.
       No breakout-aware logic (xcvr_speed_ carries explicit physical speed for cabling).
       msg: "Speed Mismatch: DevA (spA) ↔ DevB (spB)"

CHECK GROUP 2 — Node configuration:
  G. Invalid Interface Name — int_ doesn't match standard prefix regex
  H. Missing Po for Port-Channel mode — mode is po-based but po_ is blank
  I. Stale Po value on Ethernet mode — mode is et-based but po_ has a value
  J. Stale IP Type on L2 port — mode is l2-* with no SVI but ip_type_ has a value

CHECK GROUP 3 — SVI / Gateway:
  Cross-device VLAN gateway consistency (same VLAN, different GW IPs = error)

CHECK GROUP 5 — Duplicate Interface:
  Same int_ name appears more than once for the same device
  (uses globalPortFrequency server-side map: "DeviceName:PortName" → count)

CHECK GROUP 6 — VLAN usage consistency (per device)

CHECK GROUP 7 — Duplicate P2P VLAN across sheet
  Scans globalLinks for any link where either endpoint has ip_type_ = "p2p".
  Collapses Po member links to a logical identity before comparing:
    - Both sides have po_ set → logicalKey = sorted([DevA:PoX, DevB:PoY]).join("|")
      All physical child links of the same Po share the same VLAN intentionally —
      they collapse to one entry and are never flagged.
    - Standalone link (no po_) → logicalKey = link.id
  Maps each VLAN to Map<logicalKey, Set<link.id>>.
  Flags any VLAN with more than 1 distinct logical key — same VLAN on two different
  logical links → same derived subnet (oct2/oct3) → IP conflict in generated config.
  msg: "✗ Duplicate P2P VLAN <N>: Used on <X> logical links — causes IP conflict in generated config"
  Flags all physical link IDs belonging to each affected logical link.

UI: Shield icon in toolbar. Badge shows error count when issues found.
Clicking a flagged port highlights it in red on the topology.
flagErrorOnPort(pid, msg): adds msg to all links connected to port pid;
  deduplicates (includes check) so calling it for both ports on one link
  only adds the error once per link.

auditSchemaVsSheet() (server-side): checks extra/missing columns vs schema.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 17: CABLING EXPORT & GENERATE ALL CONFIGS
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CABLING EXPORT:
openCablingModal() → client-side modal in Sidebar-js.html
Exports a structured cabling table (Device A | Port A | Device B | Port B)
based on paired connections in the topology.
Download as plain text OR copy to clipboard as CSV or Markdown table.

buildCableGroups()
  Shared helper that groups globalLinks into canonical cable pairs.
  Returns { cableGroups, sheetIndexMap }.
  Used by downloadCablingReport(), copyCablingCsv(), copyCablingMarkdown().

  Speed lookup: speedX_raw = xcvr_speed_X || et_speed_X || ""
  aggX = speedX_raw.match(/^(\d+)g-(\d+)$/i)  ← aggregate format is the ONLY reliable
         QSFP-DD breakout signal. Slash notation alone is ambiguous (card/port on tuf317,
         IXIA; QSFP-DD lanes on bkd566) and must NOT be used as the sole trigger.

  Non-Arista suppression: if device type === 'non-arista', isBreakout forced false
         regardless of slash (IXIA/Spirent use card/port slash, not QSFP-DD lanes).
         phyPort kept as full port name for non-Arista devices.

  GroupKey logic (xcvr_speed_ aggregate + slash combination):
    isBreakoutA = !isSelfLoop && !devAIsNonArista && portA.includes('/')
    isBreakoutB = !isSelfLoop && !devBIsNonArista && portB.includes('/')
    phyPortA = (non-Arista or no slash) ? full port : getPhysicalPortParent(port)
    phyPortB = (non-Arista or no slash) ? full port : getPhysicalPortParent(port)

  getPhysicalPortParent(portName): strips lane suffix → Et14/4 → Et14, Et1/1/2 → Et1/1.
    Implementation: split('/'), pop() last segment if numeric, join('/').
    Bug that was fixed: previous impl set parts[last]="1" instead of pop() → returned Et14/1.
    DUPLICATED in Code.gs for server-side testing. Last synced: 2026-04-19.

    if isBreakoutA && !isBreakoutB && aggA           → "DEV_A:phyPortA <-> DEV_B"
    if isBreakoutB && !isBreakoutA && aggB           → "DEV_A <-> DEV_B:phyPortB"
    if isBreakoutA && isBreakoutB && aggA && !aggB   → "DEV_A:phyPortA <-> DEV_B"
    if isBreakoutA && isBreakoutB && aggB && !aggA   → "DEV_A <-> DEV_B:phyPortB"
    if isBreakoutA && isBreakoutB && aggA && aggB    → "DEV_A:phyPortA <-> DEV_B:phyPortB" (Scenario A)
    else (no aggregate on breakout side, or no slash) → "DEV_A:portA <-> DEV_B:portB"

  Without aggX guard: tuf317 Et3/1-3 ↔ bri459 Et1-3 (no QSFP-DD, BASE-T)
    would collapse into one Scenario C group instead of 3 individual cables.

_sortCableGroups(cableGroups, sheetIndexMap)
  Sorts cable groups and their internal links. Used by copyCablingCsv() and copyCablingMarkdown().
  1. Sorts g.links within each group by portA then portB (natural order) — breakout lane
     sub-ports appear in sequence (Et14/1, Et14/2, Et14/3, Et14/4).
  2. Sorts groups anchored on devA (left side): primary = sheetIndexMap[devA]; secondary = phyA
     natural sort (Et1 < Et2 < ... < Et10 < Et11). devA is always the alphabetically-first device
     (fixed by buildCableGroups localeCompare), so this is consistently left-side anchored.

_breakoutSides(g)
  Determines which side is QSFP aggregate (bo=false, collapsed port display, no label)
  vs lane endpoint (bo=true, individual ports shown, xcvr gets "(Breakout)" suffix).
  Primary: lane-speed format (e.g. 100g-4 on one side, 25g on other).
  Fallback (when both sides are same speed, e.g. 25g ↔ 25g):
    if isBreakoutA && !isBreakoutB → {a:false, b:true} (A is QSFP aggregate, B is lane end)
    if isBreakoutB && !isBreakoutA → {a:true, b:false}
    else                            → {a:false, b:false}

copyCablingCsv()
  Builds CSV text: header row "Device A,Port A,Xcvr A,Speed A,Speed B,Xcvr B,Port B,Device B".
  Calls handleCopy() targeting #btnCablingCsv.
  Row count per group:
    Scenario B (count=1): one row, individual ports.
    Scenario C (count>1, one QSFP side): one row per link; QSFP side collapses to phyPort,
      lane side shows individual port.
    Scenario A (count>1, both isBreakoutA && isBreakoutB): ONE row (one physical cable).
      Physical rule: splitter cables are always 1-to-N for any QSFP/OSFP variant (QSFP, QSFP+,
      QSFP28, QSFP-DD, QSFP112, OSFP, etc.): one aggregate connector → 2, 4, or 8 individual
      SFP ends. Two QSFP/OSFP connectors facing each other = laser lane split = ONE cable.
      linksToRender = [g.links[0]] → one row.
      xcvr_speed_ = 400g-4 on both sides; et_speed_ = 100g-1 per lane (not shown in CSV).

copyCablingMarkdown()
  Builds Markdown table with same columns as copyCablingCsv().
  Same Scenario A single-row logic (linksToRender = [g.links[0]] when both sides breakout).
  Calls handleCopy() targeting #btnCablingMd.

Modal buttons: "Copy CSV" (#btnCablingCsv) and "Copy Markdown" (#btnCablingMd)
  in a flex row below the two download buttons, after a divider.

DEVICE BRIDGE MODAL (#lldpModal, 480px):
  Internal ID kept as lldpModal/openLldpModal/closeLldpModal (too many references to rename).
Toolbar button: shield+lines SVG, onclick="openLldpModal()", title="Device Bridge".
  Placed in Export group after "Export Cabling" button.
Purpose: SSH bridge to lab devices — LLDP verification, device status, and future features.
  Uses a local bridge process (device_bridge.py) running on the user's machine. The sidebar
  calls http://localhost:8765 via browser fetch(). http://localhost is exempt from browser
  mixed-content policy (W3C Secure Contexts spec — loopback is "potentially trustworthy"),
  so no HTTPS/cert setup is needed. The bridge SSHes to devices with admin/no-password.
  Modal footer: "Download Bridge" (btn-mono, calls downloadBridgeScript()) + "Run Check"
  (btn-primary-mono, id="btnRunLldp", calls runLldpCheck(), disabled until bridge healthy).
  Audit row: "LLDP Audit" section label (.lldp-audit-section) + "Mismatches always flagged"
  green badge + "Flag missing neighbors" checkbox (#chkLldpAuditMissing).
  Run status: CSS spinner (::before rotating circle) + live text "Querying N devices…"
  updating to "…(LLDP done)" / "…(LLDP + status done)" as each parallel fetch completes.
  downloadBridgeScript(): embeds device_bridge.py as a JS template literal string, creates
  Blob, triggers browser download as 'device_bridge.py'. MUST keep embedded copy in sync
  with the actual device_bridge.py whenever the bridge script is updated.

device_bridge.py (topoassist/device_bridge.py):
  Run: python3 device_bridge.py. Listens on http://127.0.0.1:8765. CORS on every response.
  GET  /health → {"status":"ok","version":"2.0","port":8765,"method":"ssh"}
  Transports (set METHOD at top of file):
    ssh  — subprocess sshpass via JUMP_HOST or direct; stdlib only (default)
    eapi — Arista eAPI JSON-RPC HTTPS POST /command-api; stdlib urllib; same JSON as SSH
    rest — RESTCONF GET /restconf/data/{path}; stdlib urllib; OpenConfig YANG (EOS 4.22+)
    gnmi — gNMI GET via pygnmi; OpenConfig YANG; port 6030 (EOS 4.22+; pip install pygnmi)
  ssh+eapi: _run_cmds(ip, *cmds) runs EOS show commands, returns list of EOS JSON dicts
  rest+gnmi: separate _rest_get/_gnmi_get; OpenConfig responses normalized via helpers:
    _oc_lldp_to_eos(raw), _oc_version(raw), _oc_platform(raw), _oc_iface_status(raw)
    _gnmi_val(response) — extracts val from pygnmi notification[0].update[0].val
  IMPORTANT: downloadBridgeScript() in Sidebar-js.html embeds device_bridge.py verbatim.
    When device_bridge.py changes, update the embedded copy in downloadBridgeScript() too.
  POST /lldp   → body: {ipMap:{deviceName:ip}}
               → for each device (when JUMP_HOST set, default "bus-home"):
                   ssh {JUMP_HOST} 'sshpass -p "" ssh -o StrictHostKeyChecking=no
                   -o ConnectTimeout=8 admin@{ip} "show lldp neighbors detail | json"'
                 Bridge runs on local Mac; jump server does the lab SSH.
                 No SSH tunnel needed; no sshpass needed on Mac.
                 (when JUMP_HOST="": direct sshpass mode — sshpass must be on Mac)
               → devices queried in parallel threads (threading.Thread); TIMEOUT=15s
               → returns {deviceName:{ok,neighbors}} or {ok:false,error}
  Error cases: SSH timeout, CalledProcessError, JSON decode error, ssh not in PATH.
  Suppress HTTP log noise (log_message overridden to compact one-liner).

Client globals (Sidebar-js.html):
  LLDP_BRIDGE_URL = 'http://localhost:8765'  (module-level const)
  lldpPortStatus = {}     — "dev:Et1" → 'match'|'mismatch'|'missing'; reset on each check
  lldpAuditFlagMissing    — persisted in localStorage; controls missing-dot color + audit flag
  devStatusMap = {}       — devId → {ok, version, platform, interfaces:{FullName:{linkStatus}}}

Client functions (Sidebar-js.html):
  openLldpModal()         — resets state, calls _populateLldpDevTable() + _checkBridgeHealth();
                            Run btn starts DISABLED until bridge health confirmed
  closeLldpModal()        — hides modal+overlay
  _checkBridgeHealth()    — GET /health; on success: dot-green, msg="Running on port N", enables Run btn;
                            on failure: dot-red, msg="Not running", shows lldpBridgeCmd yellow box, disables Run btn
  _getLldpMgmtIps()       — scans allNodesData for Ma*/Management* ports with ip_ → {dev: ip (no prefix)}
  _populateLldpDevTable() — renders lldp-dev-row grid: device name | host/IP input | status dot
                            Defaults to device name (DNS-resolvable) via autoIps[n.id] || n.id;
                            Ma0 IP takes priority if present; only Arista devices shown
  runLldpCheck()          — collects IPs; fires Promise.all([/lldp, /devstatus]) in parallel;
                            updates per-device dots; stores dsData→devStatusMap; calls
                            _compareLldpData + _renderLldpResults + applyLldpIndicators +
                            applyDevStatusToCards; on fetch error calls _checkBridgeHealth()
  _expandIfaceName(name)  — maps short EOS port names to full form for devstatus lookup:
                            Et→Ethernet, Ma→Management, Po→Port-Channel, Vl→Vlan
  applyDevStatusToCards() — updates .dev-version-line divs ("EOS 4.x.y · Platform") and
                            overrides port St dots with live op-status from devStatusMap:
                            connected→op-up (green), notconnect→op-down (amber),
                            errdisabled→op-errdisabled (red), other→op-disabled (gray);
                            called after render() and after each runLldpCheck()
  _normSysName(sysName)   — extracts short device name from LLDP FQDN: strips domain (split
                            on '.')[0]) then takes last dash-segment (split('-').pop()).
                            "DUT-L-Leaf1-VG-cal423.sjc.aristanetworks.com" → "cal423".
                            IMPORTANT: EOS reports full FQDN in systemName; topology device
                            IDs are short names — must normalize before comparison.
  _normLldpIface(name)    — full EOS names → canonical short: Ethernet→Et, Management→Ma,
                            Port-Channel→Po, Loopback→Lo, Vxlan→Vx
  _compareLldpData(lldpData) — iterates globalLinks; builds lldpMap {DevName:NormIface →
                            {remoteDevice (via _normSysName), remoteIface}};
                            NOTE: uses interfaceId_v2 (no embedded quotes) with interfaceId
                            fallback + quote-strip — interfaceId from EOS has literal `"`
                            chars: '"Ethernet1"' which breaks _normLldpIface matching;
                            skips: non-Arista devices, non-Et interfaces (PO/Vx/Lo etc.);
                            statuses: match / mismatch (shows actual LLDP seen) /
                            partial (one side not queried) / unknown (neither queried)
  _renderLldpResults(results) — sorts mismatch→partial/unknown→match→skip; renders lldp-result-row
                            with inline SVG check/X/question/dash icons; summary badge (N/total)

Modal UI structure:
  Bridge bar: dot + status msg + Recheck button (lldp-bridge-bar)
  Bridge cmd box: shown only when bridge not running — yellow box with start command (lldp-bridge-cmd)
  Management IPs table: lldp-dev-row grid (device name | IP input | status dot); Arista only
  Status line: shown during fetch ("Bridge is querying devices via SSH…")
  Results: summary badge + per-cable result list (sorted by severity)
  Per-device dot: dot-green=SSH OK, dot-red=error, dot-gray=no IP/not queried

Result row statuses:
  match    — SVG check, green bg — LLDP confirms the cable
  mismatch — SVG X, red bg — LLDP sees different neighbor (detail line shows actual)
  partial  — SVG ?, amber bg — one device queried OK, other not queried
  unknown  — SVG ?, gray bg — neither device queried
  skip     — dash SVG, faded — non-Arista or non-Ethernet interface

lldpModal added to: modalOrder (Escape key), closeFuncs map, closeAllModals() list.

CSS classes (Sidebar-css.html section 13):
  .lldp-bridge-bar (flex row, bg-secondary bg), .lldp-bridge-msg, .lldp-recheck-btn
  .lldp-bridge-cmd (amber/yellow warning box), .lldp-cmd-code (bold, user-select:text)
  .lldp-field-label, .lldp-section-hdr, .lldp-hint
  .lldp-dev-row (grid: 1fr 140px 18px), .lldp-dev-name, .lldp-ip-inp, .lldp-dev-dot
  .dot-green, .dot-red, .dot-gray
  .lldp-empty, .lldp-run-status, .lldp-summary-badge (.badge-ok / .badge-fail)
  .lldp-result-list, .lldp-result-row (.lldp-row-ok/fail/part/unk/skip)
  .lldp-row-icon, .lldp-row-cable, .lldp-row-detail
  .col-lldp (16px flex col, port row LL indicator), .lldp-port-dot (7px circle)
  .lldp-port-match (green), .lldp-port-mismatch (amber), .lldp-port-missing (red),
  .lldp-port-missing-quiet (gray, when audit-missing flag off)
  .lldp-audit-row, .lldp-audit-always, .lldp-chk-label (modal audit toggle row)
  .dev-version-line — 9px JetBrains Mono, rgba(255,255,255,0.7) on colored headers,
    #64748b on plain headers; shows "EOS {version}  ·  {platform}" under hostname
  .dot.op-up (green #22c55e !important), .dot.op-down (amber #f59e0b),
  .dot.op-errdisabled (red #ef4444), .dot.op-disabled (gray #94a3b8) — live op-status
    overrides for port St dot applied by applyDevStatusToCards()

Note: Code.gs retains checkLldpNeighbors(ipMap,protocol) as a standalone server function
  (eAPI-based, for setups where devices have public IPs). Not called by the sidebar.

GENERATE ALL CONFIGS:
Toolbar button: file-text SVG icon in the Export group (after cabling button).
onclick="openGenerateAllModal()" → static modal #generateAllModal (600px wide).

Server functions (Code.gs):
  formatConfigMap(configMap)
    Server-side equivalent of client formatConfigText(). Sorts keys
    numerically, joins .full values with \n!\n.

CONFIGMAP KEY FORMAT (source of truth for both Configs sheet and tooltip):
  getDeviceConfig() returns configMap with prefixed keys for deterministic ordering:
    "000_GLOBAL"        — hostname + global template
    "001_SYSTEM"        — loopback, router general, VRFs, VLANs
    "050_<port>"        — physical interface (e.g. "050_Et1", "050_Ma0")
    "050_Vx1"           — AP VLAN SVI blocks (see AP VLAN GW section)
    "060_<port>"        — logical/Port-Channel (e.g. "060_Po10")
    "055_VXLAN"         — VXLAN block
    "070_MLAG"          — MLAG block
    "090_OSPF_UNDERLAY" — OSPF underlay
    "100_BGP_UNDERLAY" / "100_BGP_EVPN" — BGP blocks
    "999_EOF"           — configure + write memory
  formatConfigMap() / formatConfigText() sort numerically → same order in Configs
  sheet and full device view in sidebar. SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH: both paths call
  getDeviceConfig() and sort/join the same configMap.

  Tooltip per-port config: processDeviceConfig() maps configData keys to allNodesData.
  allNodesData keys are "DeviceName:Et1" (no prefix). MUST strip "^\d+_" prefix
  before canonicalizeInterface() — "050_Et1" → "Et1" → matches "SPINE1:Et1".
  Without the strip, canonicalizeInterface("050_Et1") returns "050_Et1" unchanged,
  no allNodesData entry is found, and tooltip right pane always shows "Loading...".

  writeConfigsToSheet(configs)
    Creates or overwrites "Configs" sheet tab (tab color #6366f1 indigo).
    Col A: "! === DeviceName ===" headers (220px, bold, bg #1e1b4b, text #e0e7ff).
    Col B: config lines (600px). Font: Consolas size 10.

  getAllDeviceConfigs()
    Filters getExistingDevices() → type='full' AND isVisible=true.
    Calls getDeviceConfig(dev.name) per device (sequential loop).
    Returns { configs: [{name, text}], sheetName } or { error }.

Client functions (Sidebar-js.html):
  openGenerateAllModal()    — resets body to intro text, shows modal + overlay
  closeGenerateAllModal()   — hides modal + overlay
  runGenerateAll()          — calls getAllDeviceConfigs(), renders per-device summary
  copyAllConfigs()          — copies window._generateAllText via handleCopy()

#generateAllModal added to closeAllModals() array and Sidebar-css.html hidden list.

IP CONFIG MODAL (#ipConfigModal):
Toolbar button in Modals group. openIpConfigModal(btn) populates fields from
  ipPrefs (PropertiesService). Fields stored in scriptProperties as JSON.
Legend info-box (ip-info-box): shows IP pattern with colored octets:
  .f-var (blue) = user-configurable fixed value  .f-dyn (amber) = dynamic (VLAN, Device ID)
  P2P pattern: [First].[VLAN].[VLAN].[Device ID]   Device ID = device's sheet index
  GW  pattern: [First].[VLAN].[VLAN].[Last]
CSS: ip-info-box, info-title, section-header, ip-legend-grid, legend-label all use
  CSS variables (var(--bg-secondary), var(--border), var(--text-main)) for dark-mode compat.
  (Previously hardcoded #eff6ff, #0f172a etc — fixed to use theme variables.)
Inputs: P2P (First Octet, Mask for v4; Prefix, Mask for v6)
        GW  (First Octet, Last Octet, Mask for v4; Prefix, Last Hextet, Mask for v6)
saveIpConfig() — validates, persists to scriptProperties, calls applyIpPrefs().
resetIpConfig() — resets to defaults (P2P 200//24//64, GW 100//24//64 last=1).

CARD COLLAPSE:
Device header double-click toggles .is-collapsed class on the .node element.
Single click → selectDevice(node.id). Double-click → toggle collapse.
selectDevice() shows splitDevice toolbar with Copy / View buttons. No sheet navigation side-effect.
CSS: .node.is-collapsed hides .node-body and .node-add-btn; removes header border-bottom.
Cables auto-disappear for collapsed devices: redrawLinks() skips ports whose
  row.offsetParent is null (hidden parent), so collapsed ports never enter posCache.
State persisted in localStorage key 'nb_collapsed' as {deviceId: 1} map.
Restored on each render (after el.style.top assignment in node-building loop).

EXPAND ALL / COLLAPSE ALL (single toggle):
Single button id="btnToggleCards" in secondary toolbar segmented-group, after the
3 layout-mode buttons, separated by a thin <div> divider (NOT a <span> — inline-block
span caused a blinking text cursor in the browser; pointer-events:none on the div).
Uses SVG chevron icons (14×14) — direction shows what WILL happen on click:
  ▴ (chevron-up) = "click to collapse" (initial state when cards are expanded)
  ▾ (chevron-down) = "click to expand" (shown after all cards are collapsed)
toggleAllCards() — checks .node[data-id]:not(.is-collapsed) count:
  any expanded → collapseAllCards(), button becomes ▾ "Expand all cards"
  all collapsed → expandAllCards(), button becomes ▴ "Collapse all cards"
collapseAllCards() — adds .is-collapsed to all .node[data-id], writes localStorage.
expandAllCards()   — removes .is-collapsed from all, writes '{}' to localStorage.
SVG constants: _svgChevronUp / _svgChevronDown defined at module level.
DISABLED IN SIMPLE VIEW: updateTopoButtons() sets btnToggleCards.disabled=true,
  opacity=0.3, cursor=not-allowed when activeMode==='simple' (holistic/simple view
  has no cards). Restored to normal for 'linear' and 'flexible' modes.

AUDIT-ONLY VIEW (ERR button):
Button id="btnAuditOnly" inside primary toolbar audit-group-box (alongside shield).
Class: .icon-btn (28×28, matches shield). Initially hidden (style="display:none").
Shown as display:flex when audit mode enabled (toggleValidationMode).
Icon: alert-circle SVG (circle with ! marks).
Active state CSS: #btnAuditOnly.active { background:#ef4444; color:white; }
  + svg { fill:currentColor; stroke:transparent; } → solid filled circle when active.
Visibility synced in applyValidationState() (called on init + toggle) so ERR appears
  correctly when isValidationMode=true by default on page load.
isAuditOnlyView (boolean, module-level) tracks toggle state.
toggleAuditOnlyView() — flips isAuditOnlyView, toggles .active on button,
  calls applyAuditOnlyView().
applyAuditOnlyView() — if audit off or isAuditOnlyView=false: restores all
  .node elements (clears el.dataset.auditHidden). If on: scans validationErrors,
  builds devsWithErrors Set from linkMap, hides non-error devices with
  el.style.display='none' and el.dataset.auditHidden='1'.
Called at end of runValidation() and in toggleValidationMode() when disabling audit.

ROLE PILL FILTER:
Each span.dev-label-pill in the node header gets an onclick handler (added in

Click pill → sets searchInp.value to role label (lowercase compare); if already
  set to that role, clears the search (toggle). Calls filterTopology().
Cursor pointer set via CSS (.dev-label-pill { cursor: pointer; }).

PO GROUP HIGHLIGHT:
clearPoHighlight() — removes .po-group-highlight from all .port-row elements.
applyPoHighlight(portId) — clears, then checks allNodesData[portId].details.po_.
  If set, iterates all allNodesData and adds .po-group-highlight to all ports
  sharing the same po_ value (numeric string match).
CSS: .port-row.po-group-highlight { outline: 2px solid #f59e0b; outline-offset: -2px;
  background: rgba(245,158,11,0.08) !important; }
Called: applyPoHighlight(portId) at top of selectPortOrLink() for every port click.

ESCAPE KEY (modal LIFO):
modalOrder and closeFuncs in topologyKeyHandler include generateAllModal, vlanSummaryModal,
and globalCfgModal so Escape closes them in order before resetting selection.

CONFIG AGE INDICATOR:
allDevicesData[name].fetchEpoch = Date.now() stored in processDeviceConfig().
formatAge(epochMs) → 'just now' / 'Xm ago' / 'Xh Xm ago' (relative only).
formatAgeLabel(epochMs) → 'HH:MM · just now' / 'HH:MM · 3m ago' — combines
  the fetch clock time (HH:MM 24h) with the relative age, separated by ' · '.
  Used in all green-state setSplitBtnState() callsites. Fallback to getTimestamp()
  (raw clock string) if fetchEpoch not yet set.
  Affected callsites: processDeviceConfig() (device + left + right), selectDevice(),
  selectLine(), selectPortOrLink() (disconnected port), processInterfaceConfig().
refreshConfigAges() rebuilds labels from stored data every 30s via setInterval.
  Uses selectedDeviceId / selectedLineId + linkMap to reconstruct the full label
  text ([sheetId] Device:Config:Port [HH:MM · age]) directly — avoids regex-replace
  which caused "just ago|Copy|View" bug when label was in unexpected state.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 18: SEARCH & VLAN TRACING
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

searchInp (input in secondary toolbar):
  - Filters topology to show only matching devices/ports
  - "v<number>" syntax (e.g. "v10") → triggers VLAN trace mode
  - Highlights all ports carrying that VLAN
  - Strict mode checkbox: exact match only (not substring)
  - Enter key (with no autocomplete item focused) → jump-to-device: scrolls to first
    visible (non-dimmed) .node[data-id] whose data-id contains the search text, with
    a 1s blue outline pulse.
  - Role pill click on device header → sets searchInp.value to role label (or clears
    if already set) and calls filterTopology(). Toggle behavior.

debouncedFilterTopology() — 300ms debounce on filterTopology()
debouncedTraceVlan() — 300ms debounce on traceVlan()

Autocomplete: search-autocomplete-list (hidden div) shows matching device names.
  keydown handler in IIFE (line ~8000): ArrowUp/Down navigate, Enter (selectedIdx>=0)
  clicks item, Enter (selectedIdx<0) triggers jump-to-device above.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 19: SMART POLLING
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Client polls getDataVersion() (server) every N seconds (configurable via toolbar).
If DATA_VERSION changed → fetchData(false) to refresh topology.

smartPollTimer / localDataVersion track polling state.
fetchData(forceSync):
  - Calls google.script.run.getTopologyData(forceSync, isColorEnabled)
  - On success: re-renders topology, updates status bar

SMART POLLING GUARDS (startSmartPolling — all 4 must pass before polling fires):
  1. Edit mode guard:    isEditMode === true → skip (user is dragging/editing nodes)
  2. Fetch guard:        isFetching === true → skip (prevents concurrent GAS executions)
  3. Loading overlay:    loading overlay visible → skip (initial load in progress)
  4. Visibility guard:   document.hidden === true → skip (saves quota when tab backgrounded)

BACKGROUND PREFETCH SYSTEM:
  scheduleBackgroundPrefetch() — called after render(); waits for D3 simulation
    alpha < 0.1 (layout settled) before starting prefetch to avoid lag during
    force-directed layout animation.
  startBackgroundPrefetch() — fetches 1 device config every 3 seconds;
    skips if pendingFetches has active requests (deduplication guard).
    Updates status bar: "🔄 Background caching: DEVICE (N of total)"
    Stops automatically once all device configs are cached.
  stopBackgroundPrefetch() — clears the prefetch interval (called on re-render,
    topology refresh, or when user navigates away).

  - Toggles 'dark' class on document.body

  - On load: reads localStorage and applies saved theme

All colors defined in CSS variables in Sidebar-css.html.
Variables: --bg, --surface, --border, --text, --text-muted, --accent, etc.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 23: IXIA INTEGRATION
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SHEETNAME(dummy_cell) function in Code.gs:
  Returns the name of the working sheet (SHEET_DATA).
  NOT called by the script. Used in the IXIA TAB of the Google Sheet as a formula.
  MUST NOT be removed.

Non-Arista devices (IXIA, Spirent) get only int_ columns.
They appear in the topology as nodes (labeled IXIA or SPIRENT) but no config
is generated for them.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 24: HARD DESIGN CONSTRAINTS (DO NOT CHANGE)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1. IPv6 SYNTAX: Does NOT follow Arista EOS syntax. This is intentional.
   IPv6 format aligns with IPv4 for LAB testing convenience.

2. MLAG IS EXPLICIT ONLY: MLAG pairs are declared via Device Manager (stored in
   DEVICE_MLAG_PEERS DocumentProperty). The old PO-count heuristic (>= 4 occurrences)
   was fully removed from calculateGlobalTopology(). Do NOT re-introduce any
   count-based MLAG detection. If MLAG behavior is wrong, fix the Device Manager
   declaration, not the topology engine.

3. SHEETNAME(dummy_cell) function: Must not be removed. Used by IXIA tab formula.

4. hasKey(setObj, key): Must be used instead of .has() for case-insensitive
   device name lookups. Device names in Sets are lowercase; sheet names are
   original-cased.

5. canonicalizeInterface() is duplicated in Code.gs AND Sidebar-js.html.
   This is intentional (server needs it for config gen; client needs it for
   topology rendering without round-trip). Both copies carry a
   "// DUPLICATED ... last synced: <date>" comment — update the date
   whenever either copy is changed, and keep both in sync manually.

6. generateConfig() signature: exactly 5 params (portName, d, ipPrefs, seenPos, netSettings).
   The 5th param is the full netSettings object (13 IP family flags). MUST be passed by every
   caller — both getTopologyData() (as globalNetSettings) and getDeviceConfig() (as netSettings).
   Omitting it silently drops all protocol-family-gated commands from that config path.
   generateBGP() has 8 params — settings is the 8th; all call sites must pass it.

7. VRRP is REMOVED: MLAG + L3 is invalid on Arista EOS. The guard covers all
   l3-* modes in generateConfig() and generateComplexL3Block().

8. JetBrains Mono must be explicitly set on ALL UI elements in Sidebar-css.html.
   It does NOT inherit from body in Google Apps Script dialogs.

9. WINNOW FIRST: For any Arista/EOS-specific question (protocol behavior, config
   syntax, feature availability, known bugs, IXIA integration, CloudVision APIs),
   query Winnow MCP tools BEFORE guessing or using web search.
   Use winnow_query for complex questions, winnow_quick_query for fast lookups.
   CLAUDE.md at the project root enforces this.

10. FULLSCREEN IS NOT POSSIBLE: GAS dialogs have a hard size cap (~1050px wide,
    ~95% viewport height). google.script.host.setWidth/setHeight cannot exceed
    these limits. Native browser Fullscreen API is blocked by iframe sandboxing.
    Do NOT attempt to implement fullscreen — it was tried and reverted (2026-04-17).

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 25: KEY UTILITY FUNCTIONS (Code.gs)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

hasKey(setObj, key)
  Case-insensitive Set/Map lookup. Always prefer over .has() for device names.

hslToHex(h, s, l)
  Converts HSL color to hex string. Used for device header colors.

columnToLetter(col)
  Converts 1-based column index to A1 letter notation.

normalizePo(rawPo)
  Normalizes Port-Channel name (e.g. "port-channel10" → "Po10").

getExistingAttributes(sheet)
  Returns array of attribute header keys from Row 2 of the sheet.

getColumnIndices(headers, deviceName)
  Returns map of attribute keys to column indices for a given device.

getIpPreferences() / saveIpPreferences(prefs)
  Read/write IP subnet preferences from UserProperties.

getUiSettings() / saveUiSettings(settings)
  Read/write UI layout preferences (card width, gap, refresh) from UserProperties.

THREE DEVICE VISIBILITY MECHANISMS — fully independent:

  1. SHEET VIEW (temporary, per-user) — SheetAssistPanel.html left column
     Storage: SHEET_VIEW_HIDDEN (UserProperties)
     Functions: getSheetViewHidden() / saveSheetViewHidden(list)
     Effect: hides/shows device columns in the spreadsheet only
     Used by: toggleSheetDevice, showAllSheetDevices, hideAllSheetDevices, batchToggleSheetDevices, viewShowAll,
              applyCustomView (reads getSheetViewHidden for device filter),
              refreshSheetRowVisibility (reads getSheetViewHidden for row filter),
              getSheetDeviceList (derives isVisible from getSheetViewHidden)

     SHEET VIEW FILTERS (AND conditions stacked; each filter row is a 4-column grid):
     All three filters share the same ip-section / ip-section-header / ip-section-list CSS classes.
     ip-section-list uses display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr) — items side-by-side.
     Items use device-item / eye-icon / item-name / is-hidden / ip-filter-item classes.
     All filters: OR within filter values, AND across filters. Default: all values selected.
     toggleMinimize() hides all three sections; load() fetches all three saved states.
     Dialog height 550px (Code.gs setHeight + google.script.host.setHeight in toggleMinimize).

     MULTI-SELECT (batch hide/show):
     var selectedDevices = new Set() tracks selected device names (client-side only).
     sel-row below action-row: SEL ALL checkbox (chkSelAll, indeterminate support) + SHOW/HIDE sel buttons.
     Checkbox (.sel-chk) prepended to each device-item in renderDevices(); onclick stopPropagation + toggleDevSel().
     toggleDevSel(name) — toggles selectedDevices Set, updates .is-selected class + checkbox, calls updateSelBtns().
     updateSelBtns() — enables/disables sel buttons, shows count "(N)" in label, syncs chkSelAll checked/indeterminate.
     selectAllVis(checked) — selects/deselects all visible (not filtered) items.
     hideSelected() / showSelected() — optimistic UI, calls batchToggleSheetDevices(names, hidden), clears selection on success.
     setServerBusy() calls updateSelBtns() so sel buttons are disabled while server call is in-flight.
     doShowAll/doHideAll success handlers call selectedDevices.clear() so selection resets on bulk ops.

     SERVER BUSY LOCK (race condition prevention):
     var serverBusy = false tracks whether a google.script.run call is in-flight.
     setServerBusy(on) sets flag + toggles body.server-busy class + disables bulk/minimize/sel buttons.
     Every mutating entry point guards with `if (serverBusy) return` before dispatching:
       toggle(), doShowAll(), doHideAll(), hideSelected(), showSelected(), toggleColItem(), applyColBulk(),
       toggleIpFilter(), toggleIntModeFilter(), toggleSviFilter()
     navigate() is NOT blocked (device name stays clickable) but its success/failure handlers
       guard with if(!serverBusy) before setStatus() — avoids clearing a live "Applying filter…" message.
     CSS body.server-busy rules: .ip-filter-item → pointer-events:none + opacity:0.45;
       .device-item:not(.is-toggling) .eye-icon → pointer-events:none + opacity:0.4;
       .col-item:not(.mandatory):not(.is-toggling) → pointer-events:none + opacity:0.5.
     The currently-toggling item's animation is unaffected (excluded from CSS rules).
     setServerBusy(false) called in BOTH success and failure handlers — always released.

     ip_type: SHEET_VIEW_IP_FILTER (UserProperties); values: p2p, gw, blank; 3 real + 1 dummy.
       Functions: getSheetViewIpFilter / saveSheetViewIpFilter / applySheetIpFilter
       Logic: refreshSheetRowVisibility builds devIpTypeCol map. Checks ip_type_ ONLY for devices
              with non-blank int_ on that row — prevents non-participating devices from bypassing filter.
              Normalization: ipRaw = ip_type_.toLowerCase().trim(); ipVal = (ipRaw==='p2p'||ipRaw==='gw') ? ipRaw : 'blank'
              (any unexpected value including '' maps to 'blank' — consistent with Topology View).

     int_mode: SHEET_VIEW_INT_MODE_FILTER (UserProperties); 8 specific sp_mode_ values; 8 real items (4×2 grid).
       Values: l2-et-access, l2-et-trunk, l2-po-access, l2-po-trunk, l3-et-int, l3-et-sub-int, l3-po-int, l3-po-sub-int.
       Labels: l2ea, l2et, l2pa, l2pt, l3ei, l3es, l3pi, l3ps (4-char abbrev; full value shown as tooltip).
       Functions: getSheetViewIntModeFilter / saveSheetViewIntModeFilter / applySheetIntModeFilter
       Logic: refreshSheetRowVisibility builds devSpModeCol map (sp_mode_ columns).
              Exact string match: intModeFilter.includes(sp). Blank sp_mode_ always passes (return true).
              Missing sp_mode_ column also passes (return true). Only checked for devices with non-blank int_.
       initIntModeFilter validates saved values against current item list; falls back to all 8 if stale
              (handles migration from old 4-group format ['l2','l3','et','po']).

     svi_vlan: SHEET_VIEW_SVI_FILTER (UserProperties); values: active (any svi_vlan_ value), blank; 2 real + 2 dummies.
       Functions: getSheetViewSviFilter / saveSheetViewSviFilter / applySheetSviFilter
       Logic: refreshSheetRowVisibility builds devSviCol map (svi_ columns).
              svi_='yes'→'yes', anything else→'blank'. Only checked for devices with non-blank int_.

  2. TOPOLOGY VIEW (temporary, in-memory) — Sidebar.html devVisPanel
     Storage: JavaScript Set hiddenDevices (lost on window close, never persisted)
     Functions: toggleDeviceVis, showAllDevices, hideAllDevices, applyDeviceVisibility (all client-side)
     Effect: hides/shows device nodes in topology diagram DOM only
     No server calls, no DATA_VERSION bump

     MULTI-SELECT (batch hide/show):
     let selectedInDevVis = new Set() tracks selected device IDs (client-side, in-memory).
     dev-vis-sel-row below dev-vis-action-row: SEL ALL checkbox (devVisSelAllChk) + SHOW/HIDE buttons (btnDevVisShowSel/btnDevVisHideSel).
     .dev-vis-chk checkbox prepended to each dev-vis-item in populateDevVisPanel(); click stopPropagation + change → toggleDevVisSelect(id).
     Item body click (not eye/nav/chk) also calls toggleDevVisSelect(id) — whole row is clickable for selection.
     toggleDevVisSelect(id) — toggles selectedInDevVis, updates .is-selected + checkbox, calls _updateDevVisSelUI().
     _updateDevVisSelUI() — enables/disables sel buttons, shows count "(N)" in label, syncs devVisSelAllChk indeterminate.
     selectAllDevVis(checked) — selects/deselects all visible (not filtered) items.
     showSelectedDevVis() — deletes all selected from hiddenDevices, clears selection, repopulates panel.
     hideSelectedDevVis() — adds all selected to hiddenDevices, clears selection, repopulates panel.
     showAllDevices/hideAllDevices clear selectedInDevVis before repopulating panel.

     TOPOLOGY VIEW PORT FILTERS (AND conditions; in-memory; lost on window close):
     All three filters use dev-vis-ip-section / dev-vis-ip-header / dev-vis-ip-list CSS classes.
     dev-vis-ip-list uses display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr) — items side-by-side.
     dev-vis-ip-list .dev-vis-item overrides padding to 4px 5px; gap 4px for compact grid fit in 230px panel.
     Items use dev-vis-item / dev-vis-eye / dev-vis-name / is-hidden classes (same as device list).
     is-minimized CSS rule hides all dev-vis-ip-section elements when panel is minimized.
     initApp() calls all three render functions; fetchData() non-silent reset restores all defaults.
     Post-render: applyTopoIpTypeFilter() + applyTopoIntModeFilter() + applyTopoSviFilter() called
                  before requestAnimationFrame(redrawLinks) after topology render completes.
     isHidden check in redrawLinks() posCache building includes hidden-ip-type, hidden-int-mode,
     hidden-svi alongside trace-hidden/hidden-local/hidden-global — excluded ports drop from posCache
     so their cables are not drawn on canvas.
     CSS: .port-row.hidden-ip-type/.hidden-int-mode/.hidden-svi { display:none !important }

     ip_type: topoIpFilter=['p2p','gw','blank']; 3 real + 1 dummy; section id=devVisIpSection.
       applyTopoIpTypeFilter() reads details.ip_type_ → normalized p2p/gw/blank → hidden-ip-type class.
       Normalization: (ipRaw==='p2p'||ipRaw==='gw') ? ipRaw : 'blank' — identical to Sheet View Code.gs.
       No separate validLinks filter — posCache exclusion is the sole mechanism for cable hiding.

     int_mode: topoIntModeFilter=all 8 sp_mode_ values; 8 real items (4×2 grid); section id=devVisIntModeSection.
       Values: l2-et-access, l2-et-trunk, l2-po-access, l2-po-trunk, l3-et-int, l3-et-sub-int, l3-po-int, l3-po-sub-int.
       Labels: l2ea/l2et/l2pa/l2pt/l3ei/l3es/l3pi/l3ps; full value as tooltip title attribute.
       applyTopoIntModeFilter() reads details.sp_mode_ → exact match vs topoIntModeFilter → hidden-int-mode class.
       Blank sp_mode_ always shown (classList.remove, early return) — fixes bug where GW/NA ports with no
       sp_mode_ were hidden even when all modes selected.

     svi: topoSviFilter=['yes','blank']; 2 real + 2 dummies; section id=devVisSviSection.
       applyTopoSviFilter() reads details.svi_ → 'yes' or 'blank' → hidden-svi class.

  3. DEVICE MANAGER (permanent, shared) — Sidebar.html device manager tab
     Storage: TOPOLOGY_HIDDEN_DEVICES (ScriptProperties)
     Functions: getHiddenDevices() / saveDeviceVisibility(list)
     Effect: persistent node visibility used by getExistingDevices() → isVisible field read
             by topology rendering and Device Manager UI; triggers full fetchData(true) inline in save handler; saveDeviceLabels bumps DATA_VERSION in that chain

  saveDeviceVisibility does NOT bump DATA_VERSION (Device Manager callers call fetchData(true)
  explicitly). Sheet View functions never touch TOPOLOGY_HIDDEN_DEVICES.

runFullSheetCleanup()
  Called automatically before topology read. Normalizes interface names,
  clears invalid values, enforces schema consistency.
  Active cleanup rules:
    A. Interface name normalization (canonicalizeInterface): eth→Et, po→Po, vl→Vl, etc.
    B. SVI_VLAN standardization: true/1/y/yes → 'all' (legacy migration)
    Po format normalization (normalizePo): port-channel10/PO10 → Po10
  Removed cleanup rules (audit flags these instead — user may want to rollback):
    C. MLAG+L3 conflict: was clearing sp_mode_ when po_ matched mlagConfigPorts; audit Check B flags it
    D. L3 stale SVI: was clearing svi_ when mode is l3-*; audit Check C flags it
    E. L2 stale ip_type_: was clearing ip_type_ when mode is l2 and SVI off; audit Check I flags it
    F. ET stale PO: was clearing po_ when mode is et-based; audit Check H flags it

validateAndCleanData(header, value, rowData, headers, activeSviValue)
  Called from onEdit Phase A for every edited cell. Active rules:
  - Rule 4: VLAN format validation (rejects non-numeric/range formats)
  - Rule 6: Po format auto-correction (port-channel10 → Po10)
  Removed rules (audit flags instead; user may want to rollback):
  - Rule 1: L3 + svi_ set → was rejecting/clearing; audit Check C flags it
  - Rule 2: L2 + no SVI + ip_type_ set → was rejecting/clearing; audit Check I flags it
  - Rule 3: ET mode + po_ set → was rejecting/clearing; audit Check H flags it

onOpen()
  Simple trigger: fires when the spreadsheet opens (AuthMode.LIMITED).
  - Builds the TopoAssist custom menu and adds it to the UI via addToUi().
  - Does NOT call showModelessDialog() — AuthMode.LIMITED forbids it; the dialog call would
    fail silently. Auto-open is handled by onOpenInstallable() (installable trigger) instead.
  - Does NOT call ScriptApp.newTrigger() — also forbidden at AuthMode.LIMITED.

onOpenInstallable()
  INSTALLABLE onOpen trigger handler — runs with full auth, can open dialogs.
  - Auto-opens Sheet View if a column filter is active:
      if getViewPreferences().length < getSchemaConfig().length, calls showSheetAssistPanel().
      Wrapped in try/catch — silently ignored on first run before trigger is installed.
  - Wired up by ensureOnOpenTrigger(), called from showTopologyWindow() / showSheetAssistPanel()
    on first menu use (full auth context).

ensureOnOpenTrigger()
  Installs the onOpen installable trigger pointing at onOpenInstallable if not already present.
  - Checks ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers() for an existing ON_OPEN trigger on this spreadsheet.
  - If missing, calls ScriptApp.newTrigger('onOpenInstallable').forSpreadsheet(ss).onOpen().create().
  - Called from showTopologyWindow() and showSheetAssistPanel() inside try/catch.

onEdit(e)
  Trigger: fires on cell edit.
  - Col A guard (FIRST, before startRow<3): if startCol===1, reverts the edit and shows toast
    "Column A is reserved for TopoAssist row visibility markers and cannot be edited." Returns immediately.
    Row 2: restores DUMMY_VIS_HEADER via setValue (clearing it would cause ensureDummyColumn to
    insertColumnBefore(1) on next call, duplicating col A). All other rows: clearContent.
  - Bumps DATA_VERSION in ScriptProperties (triggers client polling refresh)
  - Phase A: runs validateAndCleanData per cell (format validation + Po normalization only)
  - Phase B mode column: updates cell background colours only (po_ grey for ET, svi_ grey for L3)
  Phase B auto-clears removed (audit flags instead; user may want to rollback):
  - Was clearing po_ when mode → ET (audit Check H)
  - Was clearing svi_ when mode → L3 (audit Check C)
  - Was clearing ip_type_ (gw) when mode → L3 non-po (audit Check I)
  - Was clearing ip_type_ when mode → L2 + no SVI (audit Check I)
  - Was clearing ip_type_ when SVI disabled on L2 (audit Check I)

onStructuralChange(e)
  INSTALLABLE trigger handler (not a simple trigger — must be wired up via ensureOnChangeTrigger).
  - Only acts on changeType === 'REMOVE_COLUMN' on the SHEET_DATA sheet; ignores all other events.
  - Calls ensureDummyColumn(sheet): if col 1 row 2 !== _sys_, inserts a new col before col 1 and
    restores header, note, row 1 label, 36px width, and gray background.
  - Shows toast: "Column A (_sys_) was deleted and has been automatically restored." (8 sec).
  - NOTE: onEdit cannot catch column deletion (structural change) — onChange installable is required.

ensureOnChangeTrigger()
  Installs the onChange installable trigger pointing at onStructuralChange if not already present.
  - Checks ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers() for an existing ON_CHANGE trigger on this spreadsheet.
  - If missing, calls ScriptApp.newTrigger('onStructuralChange').forSpreadsheet(ss).onChange().create().
  - NOT called from onOpen() — simple triggers run with AuthMode.LIMITED which cannot call
    ScriptApp.newTrigger(); the call would silently fail every time.
  - Called from showTopologyWindow() and showSheetAssistPanel() inside try/catch — these are
    menu-triggered functions that run with full auth, so the trigger installs on first panel open.

SECTION 25B: PERSISTENCE KEYS INVENTORY
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SCRIPTPROPERTIES (server, shared across all users of this script deployment):
  DATA_VERSION              — integer string; incremented on every sheet edit (onEdit trigger)
  SHEET_VIEW_MODE           — 'CUSTOM' when a custom view is active
  CUSTOM_VIEW_PREFIXES      — JSON array of attribute key prefixes visible in custom view
  TOPOLOGY_HIDDEN_DEVICES   — JSON array of device names hidden from topology render

DOCUMENTPROPERTIES (server, per-spreadsheet):
  SCHEMA_CONFIG_ARRAY       — JSON array; the full ordered schema (attribute key list)
  NON_ARISTA_DEVICES        — JSON array; device names that are not Arista EOS
  GLOBAL_DEVICE_CONFIG_TEMPLATE — string; prepended to all device configs in Configs sheet
  DEVICE_HOSTNAMES          — JSON object {name: hostname}; maps device name → EOS hostname

USERPROPERTIES (server, per-user per-script):
  CUSTOM_VIEW_PREFS         — JSON array of attribute key prefixes for this user's custom view
  SHEET_VIEW_HIDDEN         — JSON array of device names the user hid from sheet rows
  SHEET_VIEW_IP_FILTER      — JSON array of ip_type values to show ('p2p','gw','blank')
  SHEET_VIEW_INT_MODE_FILTER — JSON array of int_mode values to show
  SHEET_VIEW_SVI_FILTER     — JSON array of svi values to show
  NET_UNDERLAY              — 'bgp'|'ospf'|'bgp+ospf'|'none'
  NET_VXLAN                 — 'true'|'false'
  NET_EVPN                  — 'true'|'false'
  NET_BGP (legacy)          — 'true' only; auto-migrated to NET_UNDERLAY='bgp' on read

USERCACHE (server, per-user, TTL 200s):
  TOPOLOGY_STATUS           — progress string shown in status bar during topology build
  TOPO_<VERSION>            — full JSON topology payload for DATA_VERSION=VERSION

LOCALSTORAGE (client, per-browser):
  topology_nodes_detailed_linear   — JSON node positions for detailed-linear view
  topology_nodes_detailed_flexible — JSON node positions for detailed-flexible view
  topology_nodes_simple            — JSON node positions for simple view
  camera_state_detailed_linear     — JSON {x,y,k} camera transform for detailed-linear
  camera_state_detailed_flexible   — JSON {x,y,k} camera transform for detailed-flexible
  camera_state_holistic            — JSON {x,y,k} camera transform for holistic view
  holistic_group_rects             — JSON array of group rect {id,x,y,w,h} for holistic
  nb_collapsed                     — JSON array of collapsed port IDs

SESSIONSTORAGE (client, per-tab):
  topology_snapshot_<viewMode>     — serialized render state for instant restore on reload

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 25C: GLOBAL STATE VARIABLES (Sidebar-js.html)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

KEY GLOBALS AND THEIR INVARIANTS:

  allNodesData        — Object keyed "DeviceName:PortName" (canonical). Cleared + repopulated
                        on every render() call. Do NOT persist state across renders here.

  configCache         — { [deviceName]: { data: configMap } }
                        configMap is the full prefixed key map (NOT a per-port string).
                        Access: configCache[dev].data["050_Et1"].full

  pendingFetches      — Set<deviceName>; deduplicates concurrent GAS calls for same device.
                        Always check before calling fetchFullConfig().

  selectedDeviceId    — string|null; currently selected device node.
  selectedLineId      — string|null; currently selected link.
                        INVARIANT: these two are mutually exclusive. Setting one clears the other.

  isFetching          — boolean; true while a google.script.run call is in flight.
                        Smart polling skips when true (prevents concurrent GAS executions).

  isEditMode          — boolean; true while user is dragging/editing topology nodes.
                        Smart polling skips when true.

  topoIpFilter        — Set<string>; ip_type values currently shown. Default: all values selected.
  topoIntModeFilter   — Set<string>; int_mode values currently shown. Default: all values selected.
  topoSviFilter       — Set<string>; svi values currently shown. Default: all values selected.
  INVARIANT: filters default to ALL values selected (show-all state) — empty set = show nothing.

  currentViewMode     — 'detailed_linear'|'detailed_flexible'|'simple'|'holistic'
                        Persisted to localStorage across page reloads.

  savedNodePositions  — {[portId]: {x,y}}; loaded from localStorage in loadStateFromStorage().
                        Used by D3 to restore node positions before simulation starts.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 25D: redrawLinks() ALGORITHM
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

redrawLinks() is the canvas rendering function. Called whenever nodes move or filters change.

4-STEP ALGORITHM:
  1. BUILD posCache (read phase)
     - Iterate all port rows in the DOM
     - Skip ports with any hidden-* CSS class (filter-excluded ports)
     - Read x,y from D3 node data → store in posCache[portId]
     - posCache never contains filtered-out ports

  2. BUILD validLinks
     - Iterate all declared links (from topology payload)
     - Include only links where BOTH endpoints exist in posCache
     - Links to filtered-out ports are silently excluded

  3. DYNAMIC RESIZE + DPR SCALE
     - Measure container size, apply devicePixelRatio scaling
     - Clears canvas

  4. DRAW IN 10 Z-ORDER LAYERS
     Layer 1:  base_bus      — LAG/bundle background traces
     Layer 2:  base_direct   — point-to-point physical links
     Layer 3:  non_eos       — links to/from non-Arista devices
     Layer 4:  regular_po    — regular Port-Channel aggregation lines
     Layer 5:  mlag          — MLAG Port-Channel lines
     Layer 6:  peer          — MLAG peer-link lines
     Layer 7:  trace         — VLAN trace highlight overlay
     Layer 8:  search        — search result highlight overlay
     Layer 9:  error         — invalid config highlight overlay
     Layer 10: selected      — currently selected link highlight

TOPOLOGY FILTER INTEGRATION:
  Filters (topoIpFilter, topoIntModeFilter, topoSviFilter) work by adding hidden-*
  CSS classes to port <tr> rows (e.g. hidden-ip-type, hidden-int-mode, hidden-svi).
  redrawLinks() excludes rows with these classes in step 1 (posCache build).
  This means filter changes MUST call redrawLinks() — CSS class toggle alone is not
  enough because posCache and validLinks must be rebuilt.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 25E: initApp() INITIALIZATION FLOW (client startup)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Runs once when the sidebar HTML page loads. Order is critical.

  1.  initTheme()                     — apply dark/light from localStorage
  2.  initToolbarCollapse()           — restore toolbar collapsed state
  3.  [if manager mode] → handle device manager UI; return early
  4.  [if schema mode]  → handle schema manager UI; return early
  5.  renderIpTypeList()              — populate IP type filter checkboxes
      renderIntModeList()             — populate int-mode filter checkboxes
      renderSviList()                 — populate SVI filter checkboxes
  6.  hideGlobalLoading()             — remove initial loading spinner
  7.  currentViewMode = localStorage  — restore last used view mode
  8.  loadStateFromStorage(mode)      — populate savedNodePositions from localStorage
  9.  loadGroupRects()                — restore holistic group rects from localStorage
  10. Try instant restore from sessionStorage → restore camera state if available
  11. fetchData(false, true)          — always runs; auto-verify=true triggers schema check
  12. bindGlobalSearchListeners()     — attach search input handlers
  13. initLayoutObserver()            — ResizeObserver for canvas resize
  14. startSmartPolling()             — begin DATA_VERSION polling loop

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 26: PROMPT TO RECREATE FROM SCRATCH
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use the following prompt with an AI to recreate this project:

---

"Build a Google Apps Script project called TopoAssist — an Arista EOS Lab Workbench.

PROJECT OVERVIEW:
Create a 5-file GAS project (Code.gs, Sidebar.html, Sidebar-css.html,
Sidebar-js.html, UserGuide.html) that:
  - Adds a 'TopoAssist' custom menu to a Google Spreadsheet
  - Manages network device port-mapping data in a structured sheet
  - Renders a live network topology visualizer using D3.js in a modeless dialog
  - Generates Arista EOS device configurations from sheet data
  - Supports MLAG, VXLAN/EVPN, BGP, and L2/L3 interface modes

SHEET STRUCTURE:
Row 1 = Device names (merged). Row 2 = Attribute headers (format: <key>_<DeviceName>).
Rows 3+ = Port data. Default sheet name = 'PortMapping' (stored in ScriptProperties).
Schema keys: int_, po_, sp_mode_, vlan_, svi_vlan_, ip_type_, vrf_, et_speed_,
xcvr_speed_, encoding_, xcvr_, snake_int_, desc_, sd_, dp-pp-mp_ (in that order).
Native VLAN is encoded as nv<N> token inside vlan_ (e.g. "10,20,nv100") — no separate n_vlan_ column.
et_speed_: EOS interface speed command (e.g. "25g"); used by config gen and audit Check F.
xcvr_speed_: physical transceiver speed (e.g. "100g-4" for QSFP-DD); used by cabling grouping
  and report. Falls back to et_speed_ if blank.
Non-Arista devices (IXIA/Spirent) get only int_ column.

TOPOLOGY VISUALIZER (Sidebar-js.html + D3.js):
Three view modes: Linear (cable/patching), Simple/Holistic (node graph),
Flexible (D3 force-directed). Toolbar with sort controls (SHEET/MODE/IP/ALPHA),
search with VLAN trace (v10 syntax), edit mode for visual cabling, audit mode,
dark/light theme toggle, PNG export via html2canvas, config copy/view per device.
Device labels: SPINE, LEAF, HARNESS, TRANSIT, DUT, IXIA, SPIRENT.

MLAG LOGIC (EXPLICIT DECLARATION):
MLAG pairs are declared in Device Manager (DEVICE_MLAG_PEERS). The old >= 4
PO-count heuristic is removed. Peer-links are physical links between declared pairs.
MLAG + L3 is INVALID — output error comment block instead of config.

CONFIG GENERATION:
generateConfig(portName, d, ipPrefs, seenPos, netSettings) — 5 params. netSettings (13 IP family flags object) gates IPv6/OSPF/BGP/VXLAN/EVPN commands.
generateBGP(..., settings) — 8 params; settings gates peer group emission per protocol family.
Auto-description (9-rule): physical → 'PeerDev-PeerPort'; Po → neighbor list;
peer-link → append MLAG-PEER-LINK; child of Po → append PoX.
IP from VLAN: VLAN 1050 → .10.50. Last octet = device DID. IPv6 same pattern (lab).

VISUAL FORMATTING:
Connection pairs colored by pastel hash. MLAG cells get black SOLID_MEDIUM border.
Device headers use golden-angle HSL color rotation. Conditional rules:
member ports → italic; SVI/Po/IP grayed when mode makes them N/A.

CONSTRAINTS:
- hasKey(set, key) for all case-insensitive device name lookups
- canonicalizeInterface() duplicated in both Code.gs and Sidebar-js.html
- JetBrains Mono must be explicitly set on every UI element in CSS
- SHEETNAME(dummy_cell) function must exist (used by IXIA tab formula)
- rebuildSheet() must backup/rollback on error
- DATA_VERSION in ScriptProperties drives client polling for live refresh

Use PropertiesService (Script for global state, Document for sheet-level,
User for per-user prefs). CacheService for topology caching.
All dialogs use HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile with include() for CSS/JS."

---

================================================================================
SECTION 27: TOOLBAR DESIGN — RIBBON LAYOUT (Sidebar.html)
================================================================================

The toolbar uses a two-row ribbon pattern. All structural decisions here are
intentional and documented for future sessions.

PRIMARY ROW (toolbar-row primary-row)
──────────────────────────────────────
Left group (ui-group):
  Minimize button | Refresh button | W/G inputs (card width / device gap) | O/T inputs (cable offset / top)

Right group (ui-group right-group, align-items:stretch) — ribbon sections separated by .tb-sep:
  EDIT   → editModeBtn (pencil icon)
  CONFIG → techModal (stack layers), ipConfigModal (server rack), globalCfgModal (doc+pencil), generateAllModal (all configs)
  VIEW   → vlanSummaryModal (table rows), devVisPanelBtn (eye), downloadPNG (camera), cablingModal (tree)
  AUDIT  → btnBridgeToolbar (shield/lines) + audit-group-box (validateBtn + btnAuditOnly)
  THEME  → boldTextBtn (B), themeToggleBtn (moon)
  Utility (no label, align-self:flex-end) → openHelpModal (?), toolbarCollapseBtn (chevron)

Each ribbon section uses these classes:
  .tb-section  — flex-column wrapper (label above, buttons below)
  .tb-label    — 10px muted monospace category header (EDIT / CONFIG / VIEW / AUDIT / THEME)
  .tb-btns     — flex-row of icon buttons
  .tb-sep      — 1px vertical border, align-self:stretch, margins 4px

SECONDARY ROW (toolbar-row secondary-row)
──────────────────────────────────────────
Left group (ui-group left-group, align-items:stretch) — ribbon sections separated by .tb-sep:
  VIEW  → segmented-group: btnTopoSimple (holistic) / btnTopoLinear (linear) / btnTopoFlexible (flexible) + btnToggleCards (collapse all)
  SORT  → segmented-group: btnSortSheet / btnSortMode / btnSortIp (CAT) / btnSortAlpha
  search-container (align-self:center) → searchInp + searchClear + search-autocomplete
  chk-wrapper (align-self:center) → strictSearch checkbox

Right group:
  #status div (mono-status "Ready")

COPY ROW (toolbar-row copy-group-strip, display:none):
  splitDevice / splitLeft / splitRight split-buttons + selectionStatus
  Shown only when a link or device is selected.

HOLISTIC CANVAS CONTROLS (#holistic-controls):
  NOT in toolbar. Floating panel inside #viewport, position:absolute bottom-right 16px.
  Shown only when activeMode === 'simple' (holistic view).
  Contains: groupRectBtn (Draw Group), nodeSizeMinusBtn (−), nodeSizePlusBtn (+).
  JS: _updateViewModeButtons() shows/hides this panel.

CSS CLASSES (Sidebar-css.html):
  .tb-section  { flex-direction:column; align-items:center; justify-content:space-between; gap:3px; padding:2px 3px }
  .tb-label    { font-family:JetBrains Mono; font-size:10px; color:var(--text-muted); opacity:0.65; user-select:none }
  .tb-btns     { flex-direction:row; align-items:center; gap:2px }
  .tb-sep      { width:1px; background:var(--border); align-self:stretch; margin:4px 4px }
  .right-group { align-items:stretch } — required for tb-sep to span full toolbar height

DESIGN RATIONALE:
  - Sort moved from primary (center-group) to secondary so primary right-group has room for labeled sections
  - Holistic controls moved off toolbar to canvas so they are contextual and don't clutter
  - Bridge placed in AUDIT (not VIEW) — it validates physical wiring vs sheet data
  - Utility buttons (?, collapse) have no label and are bottom-aligned to not imply a category
  - Labels are 10px muted (opacity:0.65) to be visible but not compete with icons

================================================================================
TESTING
================================================================================

Two test suites cover the pure (non-GAS) logic:

── Python (device_bridge.py) ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
Run:  cd ~/claude/projects/topoassist && pytest tests/ -v
File: tests/test_device_bridge.py (34 tests)

Covered functions:
  _extract_session_diff  — EOS SSH diff parsing (7 cases)
  _oc_lldp_to_eos        — OpenConfig LLDP → EOS format (5 cases)
  _oc_version            — extract EOS software version (5 cases)
  _oc_platform           — extract platform/model (4 cases)
  _oc_iface_status       — OC interface status → linkStatus (7 cases)
  _gnmi_val              — extract val from pygnmi response (6 cases)

pytest installed via: pip3 install pytest
conftest.py adds project root to sys.path so device_bridge imports cleanly.

── GAS (Code.gs) ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Run:  Apps Script editor → select runAllTests → Run
File: Tests.gs (34 tests)
Output: SpreadsheetApp alert (summary) + Execution Log (full detail)

Covered functions:
  canonicalizeInterface  — interface name normalization (18 cases)
  hasKey                 — case-insensitive Set lookup (6 cases)
  normalizePo            — Port-Channel number extraction (8 cases)
  isValidPort            — port string validation (8 cases)

── What is NOT tested ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
GAS-entangled functions (PropertiesService, SpreadsheetApp, UrlFetchApp) and
network transport functions (_ssh_cmds, _eapi_cmds, etc.) are not unit-tested.
They require integration testing against a live sheet or real devices.
